***мусолить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мусолить.html>мусо́лить</a> (30328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусолить.html>мусо́лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">musólitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замусолить.html>замусо́лить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">намусо́лить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wet with saliva</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave dirty marks on with dirty or sticky fingers</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend too much time (over); to discuss or to speak about over and over again</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>му́сор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">músor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>му́сора</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the pre-1917 acronym <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мус.html>Мус́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">MUS</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:московский.html>моско́вский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголовный.html>уголо́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыск.html>сыск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Moskóvskij ugolóvnyj sysk</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moscow_Criminal_Investigations_Department" class="extiw" title="w:Moscow Criminal Investigations Department">Moscow Criminal Detective Department</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́вший</a> (12572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mutívšij</span>)

***мутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a> (12572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫtiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stir, trouble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замутить.html>замути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make (water) muddy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мути́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замути́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">помути́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cloud (the mind), to dull (the senses)</li>
<li>to incite to rebel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be nauseated

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:му.html>му</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b☒.   <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>Образова́ние</a> страдального <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стия</a> прош. вр. <a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a>.   <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:замутить.html>замути́ть</a>, намутить, помутить.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мут-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мут-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***муха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a> (1648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*muxa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mows-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mus-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mew-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">múxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">insect</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>дохнут</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>múxi</b> doxnut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you could die of boredom</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ pod múxoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be mellow; be tight; be under the sauce</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> мёд</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak múxi na mjód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">like wasps around jam</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слон.html>слона́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délatʹ iz múxi sloná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">make a mountain out of a molehill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сонный.html>со́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak sónnaja múxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">like a sleepy fly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>кака́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:укусить.html>укуси́ла</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kakaja <b>múxa</b> jevó ukusíla?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what's got into him?; what's bitten him?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do bélyx <b>mux</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">till snow falls</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обидеть.html>оби́дит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on i <b>múxi</b> ne obídit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he wouldn't hurt a fly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролети́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slýšno, kak <b>múxa</b> proletít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one could hear a pin drop</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sčitátʹ <b>mux</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gape</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мереть.html>мру́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní mrut kak <b>múxi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">they drop like flies</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мухомор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>мухомор</a> (23000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морить.html>мори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">morítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to kill, exterminate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>мухомо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">muxomór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мухомор.html>мухомо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мухомор.html>мухомо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мухомор.html>мухомо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fly agaric, toadstool, death cap</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:му.html>му</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мор.html>мо́р</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучение.html>муче́ние</a> (8483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучение.html>муче́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mučénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучение.html>муче́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучение.html>муче́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучение.html>муче́ний</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>му́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sorrow, torment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:му.html>му</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 2a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-муч-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-и-тель</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

</p>

***мучить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a> (3442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫ̀čiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">múčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замучить.html>заму́чить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to torment, to anguish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">cause to suffer pain</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to torture</li>
<li>to wear out, to bore, to tire out, to pester</li></ol>

Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговорный.html>разгово́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> словообразования: мучать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-муч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучиться.html>му́читься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">múčitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измучиться.html>изму́читься</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:намучиться.html>наму́читься</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помучиться.html>пому́читься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to agonize, to suffer <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to experience pain</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to worry, to torment oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучной.html>мучно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mučnój</span>)
